        <div class="faq-header-cool" id="faq-heading-cool">FAQ KODE4D</div>
        <div id="faq-list-cool" role="list"></div>

      <script>
          (function () {
            const schemaEl = document.getElementById('faq-schema');
            if (!schemaEl) {
              console.warn('Script schema FAQ dengan id="faq-schema" tidak ditemukan.');
              return;
            }
            let faqData;
            try {
              faqData = JSON.parse(schemaEl.textContent.trim());
            } catch (e) {
              console.error('Gagal parse FAQ schema JSON-LD:', e);
              return;
            }
            if (!faqData || faqData['@type'] !== 'FAQPage' || !Array.isArray(faqData.mainEntity)) {
              console.error('Struktur data schema FAQPage tidak valid.');
              return;
            }
            const listContainer = document.getElementById('faq-list-cool');
            if (!listContainer) {
              console.error('Elemen <div id="faq-list-cool"> tidak ditemukan.');
              return;
            }
            const createFaqItem = (questionData, index) => {
              const itemDiv = document.createElement('div');
              itemDiv.className = 'faq-item-cool';
              itemDiv.setAttribute('role', 'listitem');
              const questionButton = document.createElement('button');
              questionButton.type = 'button';
              questionButton.className = 'faq-question-cool';
              questionButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
              questionButton.setAttribute('aria-controls', `faq-answer-cool-${index}`);
              const questionText = document.createElement('span');
              questionText.textContent = questionData.name || 'Pertanyaan';
              const icon = document.createElement('i');
              icon.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
              questionButton.appendChild(questionText);
              questionButton.appendChild(icon);
              const answerDiv = document.createElement('div');
              answerDiv.className = 'faq-answer-cool';
              answerDiv.id = `faq-answer-cool-${index}`;
              answerDiv.setAttribute('role', 'region');
              answerDiv.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
              const answerParagraph = document.createElement('p');
              answerParagraph.innerHTML = (questionData.acceptedAnswer && questionData.acceptedAnswer.text) ? questionData.acceptedAnswer.text : '';
              answerDiv.appendChild(answerParagraph);
              questionButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const isCurrentlyOpen = itemDiv.classList.contains('active');
                // Hapus "active" dari semua item lain (jika ingin model 1-accordion)
                listContainer.querySelectorAll('.faq-item-cool').forEach(otherItem => {
                  if (otherItem !== itemDiv) {
                    otherItem.classList.remove('active');
                    otherItem.querySelector('.faq-question-cool').setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    const otherAnswer = otherItem.querySelector('.faq-answer-cool');
                    otherAnswer.style.maxHeight = null;
                    otherAnswer.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                  }
                });
                // Buka/tutup item yang diklik
                if (isCurrentlyOpen) {
                  itemDiv.classList.remove('active');
                  questionButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                  answerDiv.style.maxHeight = null;
                  answerDiv.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                } else {
                  itemDiv.classList.add('active');
                  questionButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
                  answerDiv.style.maxHeight = answerDiv.scrollHeight + 'px';
                  answerDiv.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
                }
              });
              itemDiv.appendChild(questionButton);
              itemDiv.appendChild(answerDiv);
              return itemDiv;
            };
            faqData.mainEntity.forEach((question, i) => {
              const faqItemElement = createFaqItem(question, i);
              listContainer.appendChild(faqItemElement);
            });
          })();
      </script>
